import os
from PIL import Image

def is_grayscale(image_path):
    """Check if the image is grayscale."""
    with Image.open(image_path) as img:
        img = img.convert("RGB")
        r, g, b = img.split()
        if r == g == b:
            return True
    return False

def delete_grayscale_images(root_dir):
    """Delete all grayscale images from the dataset."""
    for subdir, _, files in os.walk(root_dir):
        for file in files:
            if file.endswith((".jpg", ".jpeg", ".png")):
                image_path = os.path.join(subdir, file)
                if is_grayscale(image_path):
                    os.remove(image_path)
                    print(f"Deleted grayscale image: {image_path}")

# Path to your dataset directory (where each subfolder is a class)
dataset_dir = "ImageNet"
delete_grayscale_images(dataset_dir)
